      git \

      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  RUN go install github.com/zeromicro/go-zero/tools/goctl@latest \
      && go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy \
      && go mod download
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl

  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.io,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  RUN go install github.com/zeromicro/go-zero/tools/goctl@v1.5.6 \
      && go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@v1.54.2
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy \
      && go mod download \
      && go build -o /app/zeromicro_go-zero
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /app/zeromicro_go-zero /usr/local/bin/zeromicro_go-zero
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.io,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  RUN go install github.com/zeromicro/go-zero/tools/goctl@latest \
      && go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy \
      && go mod download \
      && go build -o /app/zeromicro_go-zero
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /app/zeromicro_go-zero /usr/local/bin/zeromicro_go-zero
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.io,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  RUN go install github.com/zeromicro/go-zero/tools/goctl@latest \
      && go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@v1.54.2
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy \
      && go mod download \
      && go build -o /app/zeromicro_go-zero
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /app/zeromicro_go-zero /usr/local/bin/zeromicro_go-zero
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.io,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  RUN go install github.com/zeromicro/go-zero/tools/goctl@v1.5.5 \
      && go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@v1.54.2
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy \
      && go mod download \
      && go build -o /app/zeromicro_go-zero
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /app/zeromicro_go-zero /usr/local/bin/zeromicro_go-zero
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.cn,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  RUN go install -v github.com/zeromicro/go-zero/tools/goctl@latest || true \
      && go install -v github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest || true
  COPY . .
  RUN go mod tidy \
      && go mod download \
      && cd tools/goctl && go build -o /app/goctl goctl.go
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /app/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.cn,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  COPY . .
  RUN cd tools/goctl \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && GOWORK=off go build -v -o /usr/local/bin/goctl goctl.go \
      && cd /app \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && go install -v github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.cn,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  COPY . .
  RUN cd tools/goctl \
      && go clean -modcache \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && GOWORK=off go build -v -o /usr/local/bin/goctl goctl.go \
      && cd /app \
      && go clean -modcache \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && go install -v github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest || true
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      go
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests \
      && addgroup -S appgroup \
      && adduser -S appuser -G appgroup \
      && chown -R appuser:appgroup /app
  USER appuser
  WORKDIR /app
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.cn,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  COPY . .
  RUN cd tools/goctl \
      && go clean -modcache \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && GOWORK=off go build -v -o goctl goctl.go \
      && mv goctl /usr/local/bin/ \
      && cd /app \
      && go clean -modcache \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && go install -v github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest || true
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      go
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests \
      && addgroup -S appgroup \
      && adduser -S appuser -G appgroup \
      && chown -R appuser:appgroup /app
  USER appuser
  WORKDIR /app
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder
  ARG TARGETPLATFORM=linux/amd64
  ARG GOPROXY=https://goproxy.cn,direct
  ENV GO111MODULE=on \
      CGO_ENABLED=0 \
      GOOS=linux \
      GOARCH=amd64 \
      GOPROXY=${GOPROXY}
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      build-base
  COPY . .
  RUN cd tools/goctl \
      && go clean -modcache \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && GOWORK=off go build -v -o /usr/local/bin/goctl goctl.go \
      && cd /app \
      && go clean -modcache \
      && go mod tidy -v \
      && go mod download -v \
      && go install -v github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest || true
  FROM alpine:latest
  WORKDIR /app
  RUN apk add --no-cache \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      git \
      curl \
      protoc \
      protobuf-dev \
      go
  COPY --from=builder /app /app
  COPY --from=builder /go/bin/golangci-lint /usr/local/bin/golangci-lint
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/goctl /usr/local/bin/goctl
  RUN mkdir -p /app/mcp /app/gateway /app/tools /app/config /app/tests \
      && addgroup -S appgroup \
      && adduser -S appuser -G appgroup \
      && chown -R appuser:appgroup /app
  USER appuser
  WORKDIR /app
  EXPOSE 8080
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
